<name>Krystyna Bury< /name><date>1556635914091<//date><rating>5</rating>< text>
This was the first time ordering from this place, and I have to say we were not disappointed. We got the chicken and the lamb plates and they were both great. The meat was grilled with a nice char outside and still pretty juicy inside (this was chicken breast and lean lamb!), The hummus was also excellent, all creamy pitta dipping goodness where you could feel the balance between the chickpeas and the tahini. Even the rice (I usually skip the rice especially if there is pitta involved) was very well done, with a generous seasoning of spices to give it they something extra that made us actually want to finish the whole lot. Overall, all the components of the meal were done well, using simple good ingredients and seasoning. I will definitely be visiting them again.</text>

<user_id>118054140240133541152<//user_id>< name>
Rita Rodriguez</name>
<time>1523340578505</time><rate>5</rate>< text>
Order was up in 4 minutes! Fresh as can be, cold, crisp and bursting with flavor- this salad with cucumber, mint, tomato and lettuce was perfectly chopped with a zesty lemony, light vinegar flavor. Then as if not perfect already, it was topped with a more than generous 1.5 - 2 cups of lamb shwarma that was cooked perfect and seasoned with the spot on balance of spices. The order of dolma was the perfect appetizer but I think it was too much food as I left more than indulged, so share it when you go!! I did not have high expectations, since these places popping up are often pretentious and spendy, but they knocked it out of the park!  Is it bonkers that I am craving it just 4 hours after having it the first visit!? Cannot wait to go back to try the Turkish coffee selection! Welcome to the neighborhood, Truly!!< /text>

<userid>116533800107405186666< /userid>< user_name>
Ankit Agarwal</user_name>
<date>1523458143453<//date>< rating>
4<//rating>
< review>
This new place just got added to the neighborhood and its popping. I have already been here multiple times and I have enjoyed it every single time.
I got lamb platter, chicken platter and chicken shawarma with side of fries and falafel. The platter came with hummus, pita, salad, spicy sauce including rice and good amount of meat. The lamb was a tiny bit over done for my taste but my coworkers seem to enjoy it a lot. The falafel is the best one in the neighborhood - soft and not dry. Fries were good too but you only get a handful.

For the price, I would say, this is a great place, compared to the other mediterranean places around. The only problem is that sometimes they forget to give the pita or tea that you ordered and you have to ask again. But definitely give it a try.< /review>

<review>There is such a thing as a free lunch!
The 1st Aid/CPR instructor, Candy, is super-organized and uses time efficiently.  Besides being a nurse, she is a first-rate teacher. This is a great shortcut getting on and off the island but it is also very fun it only cost $2 for a car and driver an additional dollar for a passenger.  Sometimes there is a line to get on and can take a while but most times there is little to no wait.  If you like you could walk on you do not need a car or bring your bike.  Night time on the ferry is cool!</review>

< Review>
Since 1969 I have been riding the ferry at least once every summer. Other than the change in the crew, the experience and the joy of it has never changed. Riding in a car is fun, but to really enjoy the experience, I recommend walking on or taking your bike. Being out in the open on the bay is the best.</Review>

The ferry ride itself is quite enjoyable and you see the ferris wheel (quite beautiful at night), sail boats, other boats, and there are multiple opportunities for picture taking.  You can take the ferry to Balboa Island and then back.<//Review>

< review>
FAST! EASY! CONVENIENT! I was expecting the opposite to be honest. Was thoroughly surprised. About the ferry: fits 3 cars (yes you can stay inside) and many people. About 2-3 crew. 1$ per person. Not sure about the cars, I think 4$ a piece but don‚Äôt quote me on that. And just FYI, it‚Äôs cash only. Unfortunately, I didn‚Äôt have cash but my party who was on the prior ferry did. The crew member said not to worry and my friends could just pay their ferry or bring me the money when I arrived. Extremely laid back and friendly! Was fast too! Definitely beats driving all the way over there. Definitely check it out when in town!</review>

< review>
I grew up on Balboa Island and, now that I live in New York City, I make sure to get my kids down to the Island for a trip across the bay on the ferry every time that we visit (usually twice a year). We get on the ferry on the Island, walk through the fun zone (stopping here and there for an arcade game with the girls), then to the Balboa Peninsula and it the Pacific for a dip and--if the waves allow--a bit of bodysurfing! <Text>OC is known for beautiful beach fronts and  Newport is one of the best spots for a nice cool breeze by a short amusing ferry trip! You will be hopping from the island side (it is called 'Balboa island') to the Peninsula for about 5 to 7 min. ride on a small fleet that can carry up to 3 mid sized cars and 20 to 30 people at a time. It only costs a buck or two per person and a little more for an automobile. On the Peninsula side, there are things to ride as you may see from a small village festival such as wheel ride and also many restuarants for pizza or burgers.<//Text>< Pictures>

You're at the beach, you want to go on a little boat ride, but not pay tons of more for it? Ride the ferry! $1 a person each way! It's really nice to just get a drink or a snack and relax on the ferry in the ocean breeze and watch the boats. Doesn't take long either and no waiting. < Review>
Great short ferry between Balboa Island and Balboa Peninsula...love walking the area and taking the ferry back and forth. Only $1 per ride for pedestrians, and $1.25 if you have a bike. I think $1.50 for motorcyles and $2.00 for a vehicle and driver plus $1.00 extras for each adult passagers. Kids under 5 are free and kids 5 thru 11 are $.50. It's a bargain transport. Ferry runs until 2 am on Friday and Saturday and until 12 am Sunday thru Thursday. You pay your fare after you get on the boat.< /Review>
